add_namespace = austral

### INTRO EVENTS ### 1-100
country_event = { #Status of the Confederation
	id = austral.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.1 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.1.t
	desc = austral.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			NZL = {
				## Send everyone to AST
				every_unit_leader = {
					add_trait = { trait = AST_new_zealander }
					set_unit_leader_flag = NZL_character
					set_nationality = AST
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = austral.2
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #1936 Australian Labor Party Leadership Election
	id = austral.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.10 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.10.t
	desc = austral.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Curtin
		name = austral.10.a
		set_country_flag = AST_curtin_party
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.11
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.12
					days = 6
				}
			}

			
		}
	}
	option = { # Forde
		name = austral.10.b 
		set_country_flag = AST_forde_party
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.11
					days = 5
				}
			} else = {
				country_event = {
					id = austral.12
					days = 6
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
	option = { # the socialists
		name = austral.18.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_SLP_banned } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_SLP_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_SLP_strength value = 1 }

				id = austral.19

			}
		}

country_event = { #A Battle for the Trades Hall
	id = austral.21
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.21 FROM = [From.GetName]" 
		set_variable = { AST_ALP_strength = 0 }
		set_variable = { AST_ALP_AS_strength = 0 }
		set_variable = { AST_SLP_strength = 0 }
	}
	title = austral.21.t
	desc = austral.21.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # The ALP restablishes its hold
		name = austral.21.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_ALP_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_ALP_strength value = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = austral.22
				days = 16
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Lang 
		name = austral.21.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_ALP_AS_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_ALP_AS_strength value = 1 }
			country_event = {
				id = austral.22
				days = 16
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # the socialists
		name = austral.21.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_SLP_banned } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = AST_SLP_strengthen
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_variable = { var = AST_SLP_strength value = 1 }

				id = austral.22

			}
		}

		set_country_flag = AST_cnt_lead_coalition
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.27
				days = 14
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # The coalition is broken ahead of the election
		name = austral.26.c
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = AST_nats_lead_coalition } }
		set_country_flag = AST_no_coalition

			}
		}

country_event = { #The labor partie  Stabilise Ahead of the Election
	id = austral.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.27 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.27.t
	desc = austral.27.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.27.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_ALP_strength
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
				value = AST_ALP_AS_strength
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.28
				days = 14
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_ALP_wins
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.27.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_ALP_AS_strength
				compare = greater_than
				value = AST_ALP_strength
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.28
				days = 14
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_ALP_AS_wins
			set_country_flag = AST_lang_party
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.27.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_SLP_strength
				compare = greater_than
				value = AST_ALP_AS_strength
			}
			check_variable = { 
				var = AST_SLP_strength
				compare = greater_than
				value = AST_ALP_strength
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.28
				days = 14
			}
			set_country_flag = AST_ALP_wins
		}
		add_stability = -0.03
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.15 }
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.28.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { owns_state = 284 owns_state = 723 }
				country_event = {
					id = austral.30
					days = 5
				}

					id = austral.101
					days = 6
				}
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
   			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = -150
			producer = AST
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Results of the Referendum
	id = austral.160
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.160 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.160.t
	desc = austral.160.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.160.a
		set_variable = { AST_state_count_ref = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_qld_ref
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_nsw_ref
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_sa_ref
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_wa_ref
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_vic_ref
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = AST_tas_ref
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
						value = 50
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = { limit = {
				check_variable = { 
					var = AST_state_count_ref
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
					value = 4
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_arb_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_arbitration_ideas
			}
			else_if = {  limit = { has_country_flag = AST_federal_debts_referendum}
				add_ideas = AST_federalist_debts_ideas
			}
			if = {  limit = { has_country_flag = AST_commie_referendum }
				add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = -0.99 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = -0.99 }
				add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = -0.99 }
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = radical_socialist 
					long_name = AST_banned_party_long
					name = AST_banned_party
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = totalist 
					long_name = AST_banned_party_long
					name = AST_banned_party
				}
				set_party_name = { 
					ideology = syndicalist 
					long_name = AST_banned_party_long
					name = AST_banned_party
				}
			}
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_bank_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_bank_control_idea
			}
			if = { limit = { has_country_flag = AST_14_points_referendum }
				add_ideas = AST_14_points_idea
			}
			if = { limit ={ has_country_flag = AST_republic_referendum }
				AST_become_republic = yes
			}
			clr_country_flag = AST_arb_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_federal_debts_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_commie_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_bank_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_14_points_referendum
			clr_country_flag = AST_republic_referendum
		}
	}
}

# Death of John Curtin
country_event = {
	id = austral.309
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.309 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.309.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_curtinspeech

	desc = {
		text = austral.309.d.hog
		trigger = {
			has_idea = AST_John_J_Curtin_hog_sde
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = austral.309.d.nothog
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = AST_John_J_Curtin_hog_sde
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		date > 1945.7.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = John_J_Curtin_dead
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.309.a
		add_political_power = -25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = AST_John_Curtin_hog_sde
			}
			remove_ideas = AST_John_Curtin_hog_sde
			add_ideas = AST_Joseph_Chifley_hog_sde
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = AST_is_republic
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Joseph Chifley"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Joseph_Chifley.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = John_J_Curtin_dead
		set_country_flag = AST_chifley_party
	}
}

### THE NEW ZEALAND CRISIS ### 400-500

country_event = { # New Zealand leaves peacefully
	id = austral.400
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.400"
		remove_power_balance = {
    		id = AST_union
		}
	}
	title = { text = austral.400.d }
	desc = { text = austral.400.t }
	picture = GFX_report_event_NZL_coalition

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.253.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		284 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		723 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		NZL = {
			set_country_flag = NZL_voted_to_leave
			transfer_state = 284
			transfer_state = 723
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = nzl.30
					days = 3
				}
				AST = {
					NZL = {
						transfer_technology = yes
					}
				}
				load_oob = "NZL"
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment_1
					amount = 1000
					producer = CAN
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = convoy_1
					amount = 25
					producer = CAN
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = AST
				}
				add_to_faction = NZL
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_trait = AST_new_zealander }
			remove_unit_leader_trait = AST_new_zealander
			set_nationality = NZL
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = NZL_Sidney_Holland_hog_sco
			}
			remove_ideas = NZL_Sidney_Holland_hog_sco
		}
		set_country_flag = Sidney_G_Holland_dead
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.401
				days = 3
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				news_event = {
					id = worldnews.132
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		NZL = {
			change_tag_from = AST
		}
		name = austral.253.b
		add_political_power = -100
		284 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		723 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		NZL = {
			set_country_flag = NZL_voted_to_leave
			transfer_state = 284
			transfer_state = 723
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = nzl.30

# Australasia loses New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.401
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.401 FROM = [From.GetName]" 
	remove_power_balance = {
    		id = AST_union
		}
	}
	title = austral.401.t
	desc = austral.401.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_newzealand

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_war = no
		NOT = { owns_state = 284 } #New Zealand
		NOT = { owns_state = 723 } #South Island
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.401.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_is_republic }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_australia_republic
		}
		else = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_australia
		}
		284 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
				add_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		723 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
				}
				remove_core_of = AST
				add_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
	}
}

# Australia regains New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.402
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.402 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.402.t
	desc = austral.402.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_newzealand

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
		has_war = no
		controls_all_owned_states = yes
		owns_state = 284 #New Zealand
		owns_state = 723 #South Island
	}

	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = AST_no_new_zealand
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.402.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = AST_is_republic }
			set_cosmetic_tag = AST_republic
		}
		else = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		}
	}
}

# The war begins with New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.404
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.404 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.404.t
	desc = austral.404.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_army1

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		284 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = NZL } #New Zealand
		723 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = NZL } #South Island
		OR = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		NZL = { is_valid_peace_target = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.404.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = NZL
		}
		NZL = { set_country_flag = NZL_war_of_succsession }
		country_event = { id = nzl.501 days = 125 }
		country_event = { id = nzl.1 days = 1 } #start the war
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.404.b
		NZL = { country_event = { id = nzl.19 days = 125 } }
	}
}

# Peace deal - AST has captured New Zealand
country_event = {
	id = austral.405
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.405 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.405.t
	desc = austral.405.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ast_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_war_with = NZL
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		controls_state = 284 #New Zealand
		controls_state = 723 #South Island
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.405.a # It is time to call for a truce
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_political_power = 150
			ENT = { remove_from_faction = NZL }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 523 #New Guinea
						state = 636 #Fiji
					}
					OR = {
						is_controlled_by = ENT
						controller = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = AST }
					remove_core_of = AST
					add_claim_by = AST
				}
				ENT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.405.b # No! We will continue this war until it is finished!
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
	}
}

### FUNCTION EVENTS ### 500-600

# Country approached for trade deal (fired from decision)
country_event = {
	id = austral.500
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.500 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.500.t
	desc = austral.500.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.500.a #Yes - Australasia is our friend
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				AST = {
					has_same_government_as_ROOT = yes
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_accepted_trade
		if = {
			limit = { tag = ENT }
			add_political_power = 75
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		AST = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = AST_trade_deal
			}
			country_event = { id = austral.501 days = 7 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.500.b #No, we can't be bothered with this
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					tag = ENT
					tag = USA
					tag = PSA
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		AST = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = ROOT
				modifier = AST_trade_deal_refused
			}
			country_event = { id = austral.502 days = 7 }
		}
	}
}

# Country accepted the trade deal

	id = austral.501
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.501 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.501.t
	desc = austral.501.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.501.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						tag = ENT
						tag = USA
						tag = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 100
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = AST_trade_deal
		}
	}
}

# Australasia make a demand for its claimed territories (fired from decision)
country_event = {
	id = austral.525
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.525 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.525.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_army1

	desc = {
		text = austral.525.d.puppet
		trigger = {
			has_event_target = puppet_owner
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = austral.525.d.owned
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_event_target = puppet_owner }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.525.a #We have no choice - let them have the land
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
				surrender_progress > 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
				surrender_progress > 0.50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = AST
					ratio > 1.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war = no
					surrender_progress < 0.50
				}
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = AST
					ratio > 2.0
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
				faction_leader = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = AST
						ratio > 1.0
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_war = no
					surrender_progress < 0.50
				}
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
				faction_leader = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = AST
						ratio > 2.0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AST
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_event_target = puppet_owner }
			add_political_power = -50
			event_target:puppet_owner = {
				country_event = { id = austral.361 days = 3 }
				effect_tooltip = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_claimed_by = AST
							has_state_flag = AST_claimed_anderson
						}
						AST = { transfer_state = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -100
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = AST
						has_state_flag = AST_claimed_anderson
					}
					AST = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		AST = {
			country_event = { id = austral.362 days = 3 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.525.b #What? No! They will have to fight for it
		ai_chance = {
			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					is_in_faction = no
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = AST
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = AST modifier = KR_outraged }
		AST = {
			country_event = { id = austral.528 days = 3 }
		}
	}
}

# Return lands to the UK?

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.529 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.529.t
	desc = austral.529.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_army1

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		has_completed_focus = AST_the_antipodean_bastion_of_empire
		country_exists = GBR
		is_in_faction_with = GBR
		has_war = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = AST_no_return_GBR
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			has_state_flag = AST_claimed_anderson
			is_controlled_by = AST
			NOT = {
				state = 633 #Marshall Islands
				state = 684 #Caroline Islands
				state = 647 #Palau
				state = 646 #Marianas
				state = 757 #Kaiser Wilhelmsland
				state = 737 #Bismark Archipel
				state = 843 #Southwest New Guinea
				state = 669 #Northwest New Guinea
				state = 721 #Portuguese Timor
				state = 972 #Oecusse
				state = 1017 #Dutch Timor
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.529.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		GBR = {
			country_event = {
				id = austral.530
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.529.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = AST_no_return_GBR
		add_stability = -0.05
	}
}

# UK considers whether they want the lands
country_event = {
	id = austral.530
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.530 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.530.t
	desc = austral.530.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_army1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		is_in_faction_with = AST
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.530.a #Yes, please!
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				has_state_flag = AST_claimed_anderson
				is_owned_by = AST
				is_controlled_by = AST
				NOT = {
					state = 633 #Marshall Islands
					state = 684 #Caroline Islands
					state = 647 #Palau
					state = 646 #Marianas
					state = 757 #Kaiser Wilhelmsland
					state = 737 #Bismark Archipel
					state = 843 #Southwest New Guinea
					state = 669 #Northwest New Guinea
					state = 721 #Portuguese Timor
					state = 972 #Oecusse
					state = 1017 #Dutch Timor
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = AST
				}
				remove_claim_by = AST
			}
		}
		AST = {
			country_event = austral.369
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.530.b #They fought for it, they can keep it
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_approves_of_govt
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		AST = {
			country_event = austral.532
		}
	}
}

				AND = { #Both Princes are somewhere else
					has_global_flag = CAN_king_henry_IX
					NEE = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = NEE_Albert_Dead
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Albert I"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Albert Windsor"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				AND = { #Both Princes are somewhere else
					has_global_flag = CAN_king_albert_I
					NEE = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Henry I"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Henry Windsor"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = CAN_prince_george_dead
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Hore-Ruthven"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Alexander_Hore_Ruthven.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Hore-Ruthven"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Alexander_Hore_Ruthven.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Hore-Ruthven"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Alexander_Hore_Ruthven.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Hore-Ruthven"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Alexander_Hore_Ruthven.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = market_liberal_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Hore-Ruthven"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Alexander_Hore_Ruthven.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = soccon_agrarianism_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Alexander Hore-Ruthven"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/AST/Portrait_AST_Alexander_Hore_Ruthven.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.534.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = AST }
		}

	}

		}

		add_ideas = AST_civil_war_idea
		remove_power_balance = {
    		id = AST_union
		}

			521 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			522 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			988 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			517 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 284
					owns_state = 723
				}
				284 = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = yes
				}
				723 = {
					set_demilitarized_zone = yes
				}
				activate_mission = AST_nzl_sep
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Nation Stabilizes
	id = austral.904
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.904 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.904.t
	desc = austral.904.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = AST
				has_war = no
				has_country_flag = Red_Australia_flag
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = AST_war_strength 
				value = 9
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.904.a
		remove_ideas = AST_civil_war_idea
		add_stability = 0.3
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = Red_Australia_flag }
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 284
				owns_state = 723
			}
			country_event = {
				id = austral.905
				days = 40
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = austral.908
			days = 20
		}
		522 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		988 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		284 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		723 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		521 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
		517 = {
			set_demilitarized_zone = no
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Afmâ€™s Identity Forms
	id = austral.1169
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.1169 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.1169.t
	desc = austral.1169.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # left
		name = austral.1169.a
		set_country_flag = AST_afm_go_red
	}
	option = { # RIGHT
		name = austral.1169.b
		set_country_flag = AST_afm_go_white
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Adela Pankhurst" ruling_only = yes } }
			set_country_leader_ideology = natpop_popular_patriotism_subtype
		}
		if = { limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Percy Stephenson" ruling_only = yes } }
			set_country_leader_ideology = right_syndicalism_subtype
		}
	}
}

	id = austral.1214

	desc = austral.1214.d

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		OR = { 
			has_idea = AST_civil_war_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_4_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_3_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_2_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_1_idea
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.1214.a
		add_manpower = -100
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
}
country_event = { # revolution/civil conflict - factory sabotaged
	id = austral.1215
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.1215"}
	title = austral.1215.t
	desc = austral.1215.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_MEX_jesus_people

	trigger = {
		tag = AST
		OR = { 
			has_idea = AST_civil_war_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_4_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_3_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_2_idea
			has_idea = AST_revolution_1_idea
		}
		any_owned_state = {
			is_core_of = AST
			industrial_complex > 0
			is_controlled_by = AST
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 2
	}
	immediate = {
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				industrial_complex > 0
				is_controlled_by = AST
			}
			save_event_target_as = attack_state
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = austral.1215.a
		add_stability = -0.01
		event_target:attack_state = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 1.0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #faction event
	id = austral.1300
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event austral.1300 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = austral.1300.t
	desc = austral.1300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_sydney

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = austral.1300.a
		FRA = { country_event = { id = austral.1301 days = 3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.1300.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = AST_afm_elected }
		JAP = { country_event = { id = austral.1301 days = 3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.1300.a
		trigger = { RUS = { has_socialist_government = yes } is_in_faction = yes }
		RUS = { country_event = { id = austral.1301 days = 3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.1300.a
		trigger = { CSA = { has_socialist_government = yes } is_in_faction = yes }
		CSA = { country_event = { id = austral.1301 days = 3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = austral.1300.a
		trigger = { BHC = { has_socialist_government = yes } is_in_faction = yes }
		BHC = { country_event = { id = austral.1301 days = 3 } }
	}
}
